 Hepatitis: Hepatitis is a fatal disease
 hepatitis liver main sujan (liver Inflammation) kii samasya ko kehete hai
 Every year millions of people are infected with hepatitis and thousands of people lose their lives after suffering from this disease
 hepatitis ke virus (hepatitis Virus) 5 tarah ke hote hai- hepatitis e, bi, si, di or i or inaki vajah se liver ((liver) main jalan or sankraman (infection) ho jaataa he
 Sometimes the risk of liver fibrosis or liver cancer due to hepatitis also increases
 hepatitis ke virus kai baar pani ke jariye bhi failte hai
 Its viruses are very powerful which do not die easily and grow very fast
 aise main kai baar taaje fal or subjiyon ke jariye bhi ye virus kisi vyakti tak aasaani se pahunch sakate hai
 Before knowing what is Prevention of Hepatitis, you need to know about its symptoms
 purushon main banjhapan kaa khatra badha detii he ye beemaari
 
 
 Hepatitis b affects people the most
 hepatitis ke kaaran (causes Of Hapatitis) liver main sujan aa jaati he
 Care is needed to avoid this disease
 hepatitis e (hepatitis A) ke virus sharir ke baahar bhi maheenon tak ji sakate hai
 Learn here the symptoms of hepatitis and how to prevent hepatitis
 saath hi jaane hepatitis bi kyon he sabase khatarnaak
 
 
 There are 40 million people in India affected by this disease, it causes liver damage
 
 
 1
 Loss of appetite 2
 Vomiting 3
 Yellowing of the white part of the skin or eyes 4
 Fever and fatigue that persist for several weeks or months
 periods ke dauraan bhi ho sakati hai pregnent, jaaniye kaise bachein1
 Our spicy and oily eating habits can increase the risk of hepatitis
 hepatitis, monsoon ke dauraan adhik failata he, isliye is mausam main taileey, masaaledaar, maansaahaari or baari khaadya padaarthon ke seven se bachein
 2
 hepatitis ke lakshan dikhne par turant doctor se sampark karnaa chahie
 Because negligence can prove fatal in this disease
 3

 In such a case, the prosecution had submitted an application under crpc 340 which was to be decided with the illegal arms case but it was not decided on the day of judgment on 18 January 2017
 abhiyojan paksh ne dubaara court ke sangyaan main is prarthana patr ko laakar salmaan ke liye mushkil badha di he
 Earlier it was presented in the CJM court but due to the illegal arms case being held in the Appellate District and Sessions Court in rural, now this application has been presented by Public Prosecutor Pokram Ram Vishnoi in DJ Rural, on which a date has been fixed for January 10
 yadi salmaan par yah aarope sabit ho jaataa he to is maamle main bhi sajaa kaa praavdhaan he jo saat saal tak ho sakati he
 The country's stock markets fell on Friday

 The oil and gas sectors saw a boom after the announcement of approval for shale gas and oil exploration and exploitation in blocks allotted to national oil companies, and private companies to allow shale oil and gas exploration from their fields soon
 petroleum mantri virappa moili ne guuruuvaar ko kaha tha ki aarthik maamalon kii mantrimandaleey samiti ne mangalvaar ko rashtriya tel companiyon ko unhen nomination aadhaar par aavantit block main shail gas evam tel anveshan or dohan kii manjuuri de di he, saath hi nijee companiyon ko bhi jald hi apni field se shail tel evam gas anveshan kii anumati di jaaegi
 Moily had said, "the Cabinet has approved the Shale Gas Exploration Policy for the government oil companies Oil India Limited and ONGC
 " unhone kaha tha ki kuch nitigat mudde sulajh jane ke baad sarkaar tel evam gas block kii 10veen boli prakriya shuru karegi
 He also said that the government would soon resolve differences in contractual provisions

 Petroleum Minister Veerappa Moily said on Thursday that the Cabinet Committee on Economic Affairs on Tuesday approved shale gas and oil exploration and exploitation of blocks allocated to the national oil companies on nomination basis to them, as well as private companies soon
 Shale oil and gas exploration will be allowed from its field
 moili ne kaha tha, "mantrimandal ne sarkari tel companiyon oil india limited or oengisi ke liye shail gas anveshan niti ko manjuuri de di he
 "he said that the government would start the 10th bidding process for the oil and gas block after some policy issues are resolved

 is company ko baad main reliance industries ne adhigrahan kar liya or iskaa naam badalakar reliance jeeyo rakh diya

 (purv main messors imphote) ne agast 2013 main 15 karod rupee kaa ekikrut license (yuel) kaa pravesh shulk tathaa ek license vyavastha se duusari main pravesh ke liye 1,658 karod rupee atirikt migration shulk jamaa karaayaa

 isse messors reliance jeeyo imphokam ko 3,367
 29 crore was an undue profit
 ’’ Reliance Jio, opposing it, said that it was not taken any side
 company ne kaha, ‘‘ham apana kaarobaar hameshaa lagu kanoonon ke anusaar karte hai or doorsanchaar vibhaag tathaa anya niamkeey praadhikaranon dwaara tay niyam tathaa dishanirdeshon kaa anupaalan karte hai

 '' kaig kii report main chennai doorsanchaar cirkil ko tamilnadu doorsanchaar cirkil ke saath vilay karne ke 2005 main jaldbaaji main liye gaye faisle se bharti airtel ko bhi 499 karod rupee kaa anuchit laabh pahunchane ke liye bhi doorsanchaar vibhaag ko jimmedaar tehraaya gaya he
 The CAG stated that the auction rules lacked financial criteria for the bidders in the eligibility conditions and lack of condition to stay in the company, and there were loopholes such as an abnormality in terms of scope for use of BWA spectrum
 auditor ne kaha ki imphotel ne 2010 main hui beadblue spectrum nilaamee ke liye boli main adhiktar duuranchaar companiyon ko nilaamee kii hode se baahar kar diya jo data ke alaava wais services de sakati thim
 According to the CAG report, Infotel requested the network code after the auction, which would enable them to provide voice service in addition to clearance under ISP license
 tippaniyan The CAG said that dot allowed the migration of ISP licenses with BWA spectrum in 2013 on payment of an additional fee equal to the difference between the entry fee for telecom licenses and the national ISP permit allowing them to use mobile voice service using BWA spectrum
 Was able to provide
 report ke anusaar beadblue spectrum par wais telephoni seva kii anumati dekar doorsanchaar vibhaag ne spectrum upyog shulk (esausi) kii maang nahin kii jab ki is tarah kaa bhugtan vir telephone seva pradaata mukhya doorsanchaar companiyon ne kiya tha
 Internet service provider (ISP) Infotel won BWA spectrum in 2010, outpacing all in the bid
 is license ke tahat vaayas seva kii anumati nahin thi

 sansad main aaj pesh kaig kii report main kaha gaya he, ‘‘reliance jeeyo infocom li
 (formerly m / s Infote) in August 2013 paid an entry fee of Rs 15 crore integrated license (UL) and an additional migration fee of Rs 1,658 crore for entry from one license system to another
 yah migration shulk 2001 main nirdhaarit mulya ke aadhaar par diya gaya
 3,367 to m / s Reliance Jio Infocam
 29 karod rupee kaa anuchit laabh hua
 '' reliance jeeyo, ne iskaa virodh karte hue kaha uskaa koi paksh nahin liya gaya

" ’’ The company has said, "we have received all our spectrum in an open and transparent bidding process according to market prices
" isaki sharten sabhi boli lagane vaali companiyon ke liye samaan thi
 Apart from this, the rules of dot were also the same for all successful bidders for obtaining related licenses for services using BWA spectrum
 ’’ The CAG report also blamed the dot for giving undue benefit of Rs 499 crore to Bharti Airtel by its hasty decision in 2005 to merge Chennai Telecom Circle with Tamil Nadu Telecom Circle
